
1a1(ka1): / 'dus pa rin po che'i rgyud dri ma med pa gzi brjid rab tu 'bar ba'i mdo las ston pa 'od gsal lha las bab pa'i mdo bzhugaso// // / 
1b1(ka1): g.yung drung lha yi skad du na/
2a1(ka1): a dkar mu lam yongs khyab bdal/ mu sang phyo smin de rgya ha/ gang zag mi yi
2a2(ka1): skad du na/ 'dus pa rin po che'i rgyud tri ma med pa gzi brjid rab tu 'bar ba'i mdo zhes bya ba/
2a3(ka1): 'khor ba'i sems can thams cad thar par 'dren pa'i dpal/ srid gsum 'gro ba'i mun pa
2b1(ka1): sel ba'i sgron/ ma rig nyon mongs dug lnga 'djoms pa'i sman/ ye shes lnga ldan yid bzhin rin po che/ lha gnhen srid pa gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// spyir na 'jig rten gyi 
2b2(ka1): khams dang / ston pa'i sku dang / bstan pa'i bon dang / sems can gyi las dang bzhi las/ thabs dang thugs rje zung du 'brel nas/ ston pa rin po che'i mdo gzhung byung ste/ sngon gyi 
2b3(ka1): thog mar dpag tu med pa yongs la khyab pa zhes bya ba'i bskal pa byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig chags shing zhig go/ bstan pa'i sku yang 
2b4(ka1): bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung zhing s+dzogs so// bstan pa'i bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dar zhing rgyas so// sems can gyi las kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'khor 
2b5(ka1): ning bar ro// de'i 'og tu tshad med rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba'i bskal pa byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig chags zhing zhig go/ ston pa'i sku yang 
2b6(ka1): bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung zhing s+dzogs so// bstan pa'i bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dar zhing rgyas so// sems can gyi las kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'khor 
3a1(ka1): zhing thar ro// de'i 'og tu gzhal med 'd du snang ba zhes bya ba'i bskal pa byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig chags shing zhig go/ ston / 
3a2(ka1): pa'i sku yang bsam gyis ma khyab pa zhig byung zni s+dzogsso// bstan pa' bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dar zhing rgyas 'o// sems can gyi las kyang bag m gyis mi khyab pa / 
3a3(ka1): zhig 'khor zhing thar ro// de'i 'og tu grangs med mi gnas mya ngan 'das pa zhes bya ba'i bskal pa byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig chags shing 
3a4(ka1): zhig go/ ston pa'i sku yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung zhing s+dzogs so// bstan pa'i bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dar zhing rgyas so// sems can gyi las kyang bsam 
3a5(ka1): gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'khor zhing har ro// de'i 'og tu grangs med legs par bkram pa zhes bya ba'i bskal pa byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 
3a6(ka1): chags shing zhig go/ ston pa'i sku yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung zhing s+dzogs so// bstan pa'i bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dar zhing rgyas so// sems can gyi las 
3b1(ka1): kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'khor zhing thar ro// de'i 'og tu grangs med smon pa can zhes bya ba'i bskal pa byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 
3b2(ka1): chags shing zhig go// ston pa'i sku yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung zhing s+dzogs so// bstan pa'i bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dar zhing rgyas so// sems can gyi 
3b3(ka1): las kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'khor zhing thar ro// de la dbyings kyi yum chen mo'i glong nas/ lha dang gzhen dang srid pa gsum gyis bstan pa rin po che'i sgron me mdzad de/ 
3b4(ka1): skyes bu 'dul lo// kha lo bsgyur ro// 'gro ba drangs so// thar par bkod do// bde bar gzhol lo// de yan chad 'das pa'i bskal pa rim par s+dzogs pa'o// da 'di nas mar la/ 
3b5(ka1): dus 'di/ bskal pa 'di/ sred pa 'di/ 'byung ba 'di la/ gang du ming dang mtshan du gsola na/ ma rgyung chags pa'i dang po la/ ting nam mu zang gi dkyil du/ gser gyi bad ma 'dab ma / 
3b6(ka1): stong la/ g.yu'i g.yung drung bkra bar brdol te/ 'gro ba thar par bkod pas bskal pa bzang po zhes bya bar mtshan gsol lo// de yang bder gshegs thugs rje'i stobs dang / sems 
4a1(ka1): / i/ can gyi las dang bsod nams kyis/ 'gro ba 'dren pa'i ston pa la/ yab 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i rgyal po dung 'di dang / yum btsun mo rin chen gsal 'di ma gnyis 
4a2(ka1): kyis/ sngon nas tshogs bsags smon lam btab pa'i mthus/ lu dum kha ra ha sungs kyi nang nas/ sras stong rang byung du byin no// de la srid pa yi mkhyen 'brul gyi rgyal pos// 
4a3(ka1): mtshan stong gsol nas/ lha gnhen srid pa gsum gyis ston pa mdzad do// de la mtshan gyi byang bu dang po la byung ba'i/ ston pa rim gyis 'gro ba'i don la byen zhing bstan pa s+dzogs 
4a4(ka1): nas/ tshe lo brgya pa'i dus na ston pa dri med gtsug pud can gyis 'dul ba'i dus la babs te/ de yang ston pa de ni sngon gyi bskal pa grangs med gsum la tshogs bsgags/ grangs 
4a5(ka1): med gsum la sgrib pa sbyang ba'i mthus/ tshogs s+dzogs sgrib pa byang nas/ con gyi sku la longs spyod s+dzogs pa'i sku rang bzhin gyis s+dzogs shing / cer yang sprul pa'i sku ma 'ongs 
4a6(ka1): pa'i dus na 'gro ba'i kha lo bsgyur bar dgongs nas/ dgra bcom pa yang dag par s+dzogs pa'i sangs rgyas te/ lan gcig phyir 'ong ba'i thabs la brten te/ srid pa yi sangs kyi yul/ 
4b1(ka1): bar lha 'd gsal gyi gnas/ mgon btun pya'i grong khyer chen por rnam pa thams cad bkhyen pa yin kyang / 'gro ba 'dren pa'i thabs la shes rab bskyed cing blo rtsal sbyong ba'i 
4b2(ka1): tshul mdzad de bzhugs na/ tche lo stong pa'i ston pas stong dpal gyi 'byor pa can gyis 'gro don mdzad nas/ rtag tu re ba'i sems can rnams la sun dbyung ba'i phyir/ mi rtag 
4b3(ka1): mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshul bstan te/ 'og cin gyi gnas su gshegs pa'i dus su/ gzung khye' gsal ba la gsungs pa/ nyon cig khye' gsal bsnton/ blo gsal 'cho med 
4b4(ka1): gtsug pud khyod/ lud 'bar gtsug skyes dri ma med/ bskal bzang 'gro ba 'dren pa'i gzhen/ tshe rabs gong nas sgrib sbyangs shing / bskal 'id gong nas tshigs bsags pas/ 
4b5(ka1): tshogs s+dzogs sgrib sbyangs nus mthu yis/ bskal bzang sangs rgyas sa ru slabs/ dbyings na bzhugs dang mkha' la byon/ dog la sems can don mdzad pa/ gzhan dbang mi 'gyur 
4b6(ka1): rang dbang can/ 'gro don ci ltar byas kyang btub/ gzung la brtsi ba'i gcen po nga/ tshe lo stong pa'i ston par song / 'khor ba'i sems can mtha' med la/ gnam gyi skar ma 
5a1(ka1): / b/ tsam zhig drangs/ rtsi yi mchog ma tsam zhig lus/ chab kyi gram pa tsam zhig drangs/ chang dar sang ma tsam zhig lus/ 'gro ba sems can don ched la/ thang 
5a2(ka1): chadg al dub yod pa dang / yid chad skyeid lug ma lags te/ 'gro ba 'dren pa'i ston pa rnams/ bskal pa ya thog ring po dang / mthog tha ma thung dun dang / bar gyi bskal pa'i / 
5a3(ka1): kzhugs so la/ gang 'dul rim gyis 'gro 'dul phyir/ 'dren pa'i ston pa rim gyis 'byung / bdag kyang 'gro don cher grub nas/ sud na lus pa'i 'gro ba rnams/ rtag par sun dbyung 
5a4(ka1): dper bstan dang / dge la dad brtson bskyed phyir du / mi rtag mya ngan 'das tshul bstan/ yang dag grub pa'i gnas su 'gro/ 'og min 'da' ba med par bzhugs/ tshe lo stong pa'i 
5a5(ka1): bstan s+dzogs nas/ da lha brgya la shar ba'i dus/ khyod kyis 'gro don dus la babs/ gcen gyis bskoMs pa ci bzhin du/ khyod ni 'gro ba'i don la song / 'og men lha yi po brang du // / 
5a6(ka1): s+dzogs sku gnhen lha 'd dkar dang / sred pa yi sangs yul du ni/ gti rabs sangs po 'bum khri dang / mgon btsun pbya yi grong khyer du / 'gro ba 'dren pa'i gzhen khyod nyid/ bstan / 
5b1(ka1): pa gcig la gnas pa'i phyir/ thabs dang thugs rje zung du 'brel/ sems can 'gro ba 'dul ba mdzod/ ces gsungs so// de la blo gsal 'chi med gtsug pud kyis zhus pa// 
5b2(ka1): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ston pa lags/ 'gro ba 'dul ba'i yab gcig po/ gang 'dul der ston dpal gyi 'byor/ nam mkha'i bdag po 'di stong can/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor kun 
5b3(ka1): mdzes pa/ 'gro ba'i don grub ngo mtshar che/ sems can don mdzad rjes yi rang / mkhyen ldan nyid la bdag bstod do// nyid kyi zhal nas gsung byin pa/ gcen gyis bka' 
5b4(ka1): gnyan gcig mi rlung / bskal pa mar 'grib dus yin te/ bdag ni 'gro ba'i don la 'gro/ sems can gdul bya ci ltar bya/ 'gro don smon lam ci ltar 'debs/ nyid kyis 
5b5(ka1): bka' gnang mdzad du gsol/ zhes zhus so// de la ston pas bka' stsal pa/ nyon cig ud 'bar gtsug skyes nyon/ sems can thar par bkod pa la/ 'gro ba rang mthun / 
5b6(ka1): cha lugs sprul/ yab kyi sta dang yum gyi lhum/ rgyal rigs dra ma'i gdung la zhugs/ gzhon nu rol rtsed mdzad tshul dang / rgyal bus rgyal s gnon tshul dang / bstan pa 
6a1(ka1): byb/ phyogs bcur se la tshul dang / khab kyi dpal 'bar bzhes tshul dang / 'gro ba thar par drang tshul dang / bdud btul bar chad bsal tshul dang / bstan pa rjes su bzhag / 
6a2(ka1): tshul dang / khyamsng rab 'byung tshul dang / 'thor ypang dgon pa mnad tshul dang / me tag myangan 'das tshul lo// phyir yang 'bro ba'i don ced du/ thad med bn la yid gzungs 
6a3(ka1): shing / pha rol phyin pa bcu ldan te/ 'phrin las rnam bzhir rgyun zhugs nas/ gang la gang 'dul de ston gyis/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen par mdzod/ 'gro don dpag med 
6a4(ka1): 'grub nas kyang / yang dag grub pa'i gnas su shog/ bon nyid dbyings su mdzal bar bya/ zhes gsungs nas/ 'gro ba 'dul ba'i dbang bskur lung gnang nas 'og min du gshegs 
6a5(ka1): so// de nas blo gsal 'tsha med gtsug pud ces bya ba des/ ston pas stong dpal 'byor gyis bka' gnang ba dang / tshe lo brgya pa'i 'gro ba 'dul ba'i dus la babas par dgongs nas/

6b2(ka1): lags/ nyid kyi thugs rjes yongs la khyab/ mkhyen dang brtse ba'i bdag nyid can/ ston pa sa stong dpal 'byor gyis/ 'gro ba sems can don s+dzogs nas/ gshegs pa'i bshul / 
6b3(ka1): khar bdag las su/ sems can don la song zhig gsungs/ bdag gis dus la babs lags sam/ 'dul na gdul bya ci ltar 'dul/ rje yis bka' gnang mdzad du gsol//

6b5(ka1): pa dpag tu med pa nas/ da lha'i bskal pa bzang po 'di nyid bar du / 'jig rten gyi khams kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig chags shing zhig go/ ston pa'i sku yang bsam gyis ma 
6b6(ka1): khyab pa zhig byung zhing s+dzogs so// bstan pa'i bon kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dar zhing rgyas so// mdzad pa'i 'phrin las kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig bkod cing spel / 
7a1(ka1): h/ lo// sems can gyi las kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'khor zhing thar ro// de yang dbyings kyi yum chen mo'i klong nas/ lha gnhan srid pa gsum res thabs dang / 
7a2(ka1): thugs rje zung du brel nas/ 'gro basems can gyi don mdzad cing s+dzogs so// ddus 'd/ bskal pa 'di/ sred pa 'di/ 'byung ba 'di la/ lha gang gis thugs rjes 'dzin pa dang / 
7a3(ka1): gzhen gang gis bstan pa mdzad pa dang / sred pa gang gis rgyud sel ba dang / 'gro ba ci ltar 'dul na/ lha bdag dang gnhen khyod nyid dang srid pa sangs po 'brum khri dang gsum gyis/ 'gro /

7a6(ka1): ba kun gyi pha mar dgongs nas/ srid pa yi sangs kyi gnas na bzhugs shing / phyi snod dang nang bcud chags shing 'phel ba dang dar zhing rgyas par mdzad de/ bstan pa sel ba'i gzhi ma 
7b1(ka1): gtings so// gzhen khyod nyid ni cer yang sul pa'i sku zhes bya ba yin pas/ 'gro basems can gyi don la bya'i grong kbyer chen po ru blo byong zhing / bar lha 'd gsal gyi gnas

7b5(ka1): rje'i yul du go mnyam pas/ gang gi yul du gshegs pa lags/ 'gro dug rang mthun cha lugs la/ skye ba bzhi la brten dgos pas/ skye gnas gang du 'khrungs pa lags/ 
7b6(ka1): rigs la bzang ngan bye brag rnams/ bon nyid klong du do mnyam pas/ so sor 'dam ga 'thad lags sam/ g.yung drung sku la nam mkha'i tshe/ srog med bdud dang bral lags nas/ skye 
8a1(ka1): @/ 'che rang dbang che lags te/ sngon gyi ston pa'i dpe bzhin du/ m rtag dper bstan dus nam lags/ zhes zhus so// de la yang bka' stsal pa/ nyon cig khye'u blo /

8a3(ka1): tu thabs dang rten 'brel 'dzom dgos pa yin pas/ 'gro ba rigs drug gi gnas nas kyang / lha'i yul du ston pa la ma gshegs shig/ lha rnams ni longs spyod 'du 'dzi yais ni 
8a4(ka1): g.yeng / g.yeng skying gi le lo na che/ brtson 'grus kyigs pa ni zhan/ rang bslu' 'dod yin gyis g.yengs nas bstan pa'i bon la nyan mi khom pas/ ston pa'i sgron ma 
8a5(ka1): gshegs pa'i gnas ma lags so// lha ma yin gyi gnas su ston pa ma gshegs zshig/ lha ma yin rnams ni 'thab rtsod kyi sdug bsngal ni che/ bsad bcad kyi las la ni 
8a6(ka1): brtson/ go khrab dang mtshon cha'i longs spyod ni bsags/ rang chesng rgyal gyi dbang du gyur nas bstan pa'i bon la nyan mi khom pas/ ston pa'i sgron ma gshegs pa'i gnas ma 
8b1(ka1): lags so// mtha' 'khob kyi gnas su ston pa'i sbron ma ma gzhegs zhig/ mtha' 'khob kyi mi rnams ni phrag dag gi btsin ra ni dam/ sdug bsngal gyi 'dod pas zni gdungs/ 
8b2(ka1): brel 'pongs kyi las la g.yengs nas/ bstan pa'i bon la nyan mi tkshom pas/ ston pa'i khron ma gzhegs pa'i gnas ma lagsso// byil song g yul du sten pa'i phron ma ma 
8b3(ka1): gshegs shig/ byil sog rnams ni gti mug gi mun pas gtibs/ blin lhugs kyi sdug bsngal ni myong / gcig la gcig gnod gcig la gcig 'tcho zhing / chang dar gyi 
8b4(ka1): thang ma'i tshul du gnas pas/ bstan pa'i bon nyan mi khom pas/ ston pa'i sgron ma gshegs pa'i gnas ma lags so// yi dgs kyi yul du ston pa ma gshegs shig/ ya 
8b5(ka1): dgas rnams ni 'dod chags kyi chu bo na 'byub/ bkres skom gyi sdug bsngal gyis ni gdungs/ zhen chags kyi rgya mtsor byeng nas bstan pa'i bon la nyan mi khom pas/ ston 
8b6(ka1): pa'i sgron ma gshegs pa'i gnas ma lags so// dmyal ba'i yul du ston pa ma gshegs shig/ dmyal ba rnams ni zhe sdang gi me chen ni 'bar/ tsha grang gi sdug bsngal gyis 
9a1(ka1): ni sbying / btsoM bsreg gi las ni brtson nas bstan pa'i bon la nyan mi khom pas/ sten pa'i sgron ma gshegs pa'i gnas ma lags so// skye ba rnam pa bzhi la /

10a1(ka1): grags pa che ba/ s+dzu 'brul gyi sku gcig tu spul la gshegs zhig/ rigs ni bdag gis byin gyis brlabs shing / 'gro ba yongs la bka' btsan pa/ dmu rigs /

10b1(ka1): 'jig nyen gyi khams gang bar rgyud la yongs su byin gyis brlabs so// lha yis kyang sprul pa byung bas/ ya ki dbu'i gtsug ter nas/ ma ki zhabs kyi long bu yan chad du/ yi 
10b2(ka1): shes dbyings kyi lha dang / rigs lnga'i sangs rgyas dang / phyogs bcu' bad bar gzhegs pa yi gzen sems dpa' dang sems masgo ba dang sgo ma/ thugs rjes sprul pa'i lha dang / ru bzhi
